U.S. Silver Policy

(New York) According to highly reliable sources, Congress will not legislate to make the U.S. currency a bimetallic standard. The authorities' will remains strictly secret, but judging from the current situation, the government is currently confiscating silver and prohibiting exports and imports in accordance with the gold method, and will probably pay 5 jiao per ounce to deal with the current speculative supply to the government, or even increase the price of new mined silver until the ratio of gold to silver reaches 1 to 16. Then the government may issue silver certificates according to the amount of silver confiscated and allow these new silver certificates to be used to purchase cash silver. (22nd Guomin Dispatch)

Topeka Democratic Senator McGill spoke here today, advocating the use of gold and silver as the standard for the U.S. currency, saying that minting coins with silver would increase the price of silver, and that the purchasing power of silver-using countries in South America and the Far East would increase accordingly, and that it would be on par with the United States, so the United States' declining foreign trade would benefit greatly. (22nd Guomin Dispatch)

Belgium's New King Sworn In

Leopold III Becomes the Fourth Monarch Since the Nation's Founding

Pledge to Abide by Constitution and Civil Law

To Uphold the Independence of the Nation

Brussels – New King Leopold III, escorted by troops, proceeded from the Laeken Palace to the Parliament this morning to take the oath of allegiance to the Constitution. The streets were lined with spectators, who cheered "Long live the new King!" Upon arriving at the Parliament, Leopold III, before members of both houses and the royal family, swore to uphold the Constitution and civil law, and to safeguard the nation's independence and territorial integrity. He then addressed the assembly, stating that he would emulate his ancestors in serving the country, strive for unity among all classes according to his father's intentions, and promote the development of the colonies. He also said that Belgium would continue to participate in peaceful endeavors. The new king first spoke in French, then repeated the speech in Flemish. He then withdrew amidst the cheers of the public, concluding the ceremony. Although the conflict in the Parliament last night and the pronouncements of the Flemish National Party and the Communist Party raised fears of disturbances today, the enthronement ceremony proceeded quietly, without incident. It is noted that the Flemish National Party claimed that the Belgian royal family had never taken any action to protect the special interests of the Flemish people, while the Communist Party stated that the death of the former King Albert was not entirely accidental. Upon hearing these statements, the assembly argued and even exchanged blows. (Reuter, 23rd)

Brussels – When the new King stated in his address that he was determined to serve the country, the entire assembly rose to its feet and cheered enthusiastically. The new Queen was so moved that she shed tears. The funeral of the late King yesterday was delayed by half an hour to allow retired soldiers to pass by the King's coffin and pay their final respects. The public is now praising the new King's benevolence. Furthermore, the new King canceled the customary reception for the public in the capital on the day after the new monarch's enthronement. Instead, he drove through streets crowded with people for twelve miles, deeply moving the public. (Reuter, 23rd)

Brussels – Crown Prince Leopold is scheduled to succeed his late father today as King, taking the title Leopold III, thus opening a new chapter in Belgian history. He is the fourth monarch since the founding of Belgium. Initially, Belgium was part of the Netherlands. In 1830, it declared its independence and formed an independent nation. In June of the following year, the first monarch ascended the throne.

At 8:00 AM this morning (approximately 4:00 PM Shanghai time), all church bells will ring, and a 111-gun salute will be fired. An hour later, the Chief of Staff of the Army will pay respects to the new King outside the Laeken Palace. This will be followed by the renowned Mayor of Brussels, Max, and various councilors. Subsequently, the new King and Queen, along with the Queen Mother, will proceed to the Parliament by car. Afterward, another 111-gun salute will be fired. As the oath of enthronement is read, a third 111-gun salute will be fired, thus concluding the ceremony. Traditionally, on the day after the new monarch's enthronement, people from all directions would gather in the capital to express their love and support. Now, at the Crown Prince's request, this custom has been canceled. (Reuter, 23rd)

Chairman Lin Sends Congratulatory Telegram

(Nanjing) – Upon the accession of Belgium's new King Leopold on the morning of the 23rd, Chairman Lin sent a special telegram of congratulations, and appointed Gu Weijun and Zhang Naiyan as special envoys to convey the congratulations. The original telegram read: "To His Majesty Leopold III, King of Belgium, upon the auspicious occasion of Your Majesty's enthronement, I, as Chairman, on behalf of the Republic of China, extend my sincere congratulations and wish for harmonious Sino-Belgian relations, Your Majesty's healthy governance, and the prosperous destiny of Belgium." (Central News Agency, 23rd)

Military Disarmament Discussions Show Full Understanding Between Britain and Germany

Germany Claims No Desire to Rebuild Military

Raises Reservations on British Plan

Eden Completes Mission and Departs Germany for Italy

(Berlin) – The discussions on military disarmament between the British Lord Privy Seal Anthony Eden, and the German Chancellor Hitler and Foreign Minister Neurath, concluded today. This afternoon, the German authorities issued the following communiqué:

"The discussions between the British Lord Privy Seal, Lord Eden, and the German authorities regarding the issue of military disarmament have concluded today. Lord Eden had lengthy discussions with Chancellor Hitler twice, and also met with Foreign Minister Neurath several times. Both sides demonstrated a spirit of sincerity and friendship, and expressed the desire of both governments to reach a general agreement on this issue as soon as possible. Although the purpose of these discussions was not to reach a concrete agreement on the content of a disarmament treaty, the joint exploration has led to a full understanding of the issue. Therefore, it is felt that although there are still many obstacles on the road to concluding a disarmament treaty, some progress has been made."

According to reliable sources, Hitler and Neurath repeatedly stated during the discussions that Germany had no desire to rebuild its military but maintained that Germany should be allowed to possess defensive weapons. If so, Germany would be willing to give up offensive weapons, and the same applies to aircraft. However, Hitler said that he would be willing to accept control and make the Brown Shirts non-military in nature, but other countries would also have to accept the same control. Germany is prepared to agree to a short-term military service of 300,000 militiamen and supports any disarmament plan that other countries are prepared to implement. Eden met with President Hindenburg today and is scheduled to depart for Rome tomorrow morning to hold talks with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and others, and then plans to visit Paris again to continue discussions with French Prime Minister Doumergue and others. (Reuter, 22nd)

(Berlin) – The visit of Mr. Eden to Germany to discuss disarmament issues with key German government officials has now come to an end. A semi-official political and diplomatic report here states that the outcome of the Anglo-German talks was "absolutely satisfactory." The report, from a semi-official German foreign ministry organ, states that "Mr. Eden's mission to Germany is now complete. Both sides have clarified their fundamental views on the issue of disarmament. The failure to reach a concrete agreement at this open and sincere meeting is not problematic, as Mr. Eden came here with a special mission from the British government. Although Germany has not unconditionally accepted the British plan in its entirety, and there are still differences of opinion on issues such as the air force and the duration of the disarmament agreement, these minor points are not of crucial importance. The final solution will have to wait until the draft treaty is submitted, and the interests and demands of the major powers are clarified before its feasibility can be determined. However, the most important result of Mr. Eden's negotiations is that the British Lord Privy Seal left Germany with a clear understanding of the new German state, namely, that the path followed by the new Germany will not endanger world peace, nor will it leave the now heavily armed nations unable to disarm themselves. Mr. Eden has a very clear understanding of the German government's objective, which is merely to create a preliminary position of security and equality for Germany. However, fundamental differences of opinion continue to exist today, and the time is not yet ripe for a disarmament conference or a mediation meeting, as any meeting would be futile if the final goals are not aligned. It is hoped that Mr. Eden will gather more information on his trip to Italy, and that a decision will be made when he returns to Paris." (National Telegram, 22nd)

(Berlin) – After spending three days in Berlin to complete his mission, the British Lord Privy Seal, Mr. Eden, departed for Rome this morning. The British Ambassador and key German government officials saw him off at the station. (National Telegram, 23rd)

(London) – Rumors of the situation surrounding Eden's talks in Berlin have made people somewhat optimistic about the current situation. People here are taking a reserved attitude towards this news. Generally speaking, Germany may accept certain points of the British memorandum but has attached some conditions, and if these conditions are accommodated, it would be enough to greatly alter the British memorandum. The extent to which Germany's proposals can be adopted will have to await Eden's return home and a decision by the Cabinet. (Havas, 22nd)

Revenge Marchers Set Off for London

Singing Revolutionary Songs Along the Way

Opposing the "Means Test"

Police Authorities Prepare for Precautions

(London) – The so-called "Revenge Marchers" are expected to arrive in London at the end of this week. As a preventative measure, the police authorities are recruiting temporary police to maintain order. Currently, 20,000 civilians have responded to the call, and it is expected that at least 10,000 will be assigned to patrol duties, most of whom will be stationed in Hyde Park. Stores around Hyde Park are now taking special precautions to protect their property. (National Telegram, 22nd)

(London) – Today, 2,000 unemployed people set off from various parts of Britain for London, singing along the way, "When the time of revolution arrives, we will hang MacDonald on the sour apple tree." This march is organized by the Communist Party and the Independent Labour Party and will hold a demonstration in Hyde Park on Monday of next week. This march is different from the hunger march of December 1932. Its purpose is to oppose the police oppression, forced labor, and various other aspects of the unemployment issue. What they resent most is the so-called "means test," which forces those receiving unemployment benefits to prove that they have no means of making a living. They all point out that this regulation is tantamount to swearing an oath of poverty. The marchers, both men and women, are selected for their physical strength and ability to withstand the elements. They all carry cooking utensils and other items. The London police authorities are now taking all precautions to avoid a riot like the previous march. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Nicaraguan Revolutionary Leader Sandino Assassinated

Perpetrated by Members of the National Guard

Fears of Civil War Arise

National Martial Law Declared

Managua – General Sandino, the leader of the 1932 revolution in Nicaragua, Central America, was assassinated last night outside the city. His brother Socrates and Generals Estrada and others were also killed. Sandino came to the capital to discuss the future of the Nicaraguan National Guard with Nicaraguan President Sacasa. Sandino would dismiss his own troops, on the condition the National Guard would be reorganized. The President had strictly ordered his subordinates to protect Sandino and others' safety while they were in the capital, but these orders were not followed, and Sandino and others were brutally murdered. The President was furious and ordered an immediate investigation and asked the Congress to provide facilities for maintaining public order. Sandino's followers will undoubtedly be resentful upon hearing this tragic news, and it is feared that Nicaragua will once again descend into civil war. The murderers have not yet been apprehended, but there is no doubt that the incident was perpetrated by members of the National Guard. The President has now ordered that all correspondence be subject to strict censorship. (Reuters, 22nd)

Managua – Since the assassination of General Sandino, leader of the Revolutionary Party, martial law has been declared throughout the country. General Sandino, along with Generals Estrada and Umanzor, were returning after having dinner with the President when soldiers of the National Guard blocked the road and forced the three onto a truck, driving them to the airfield, where they were stood up and shot to death with machine guns. Soon after, Sandino's brother Socrates also suffered the same fate. It is said that President Sacasa was not involved in this atrocity, as he had always shown great respect for General Sandino. (Reuter, 23rd)

South Irish Parliament Passes Law Banning Blue Shirts

Unexpected by Opposition Parties

Raucous Scene in Parliament

Dublin – The South Irish Parliament today passed the first reading of the law banning the wearing of blue shirts by a vote of 65 to 40. The introduction of the bill for the first reading was unexpected by the opposition parties, causing a great uproar. Although the bill does not specifically mention General O'Duffy's Blue Shirt Army, its purpose is undoubtedly to ban the group. The bill is titled "Law Banning the Wearing or Carrying of Uniforms, Armbands, Insignia, etc." When Minister of Justice Ruttledge introduced the bill, he stated that the government believed that previous breaches of peace were related to militarization and politics. The bill aims to end this kind of evil and maintain peace and order. The assembly responded with jeers. Then, Dr. Walshingtons (whose brother was murdered while serving as an administrator in the Cosgrave government) rose to say that this bill was purely political in nature and was intended to subject those who dared to oppose the head of administration to legal punishment. At this, the crowd shouted wildly, and several members of De Valera's party rose up and angrily denounced it. Ministry of Railways Plans to Reroute the Nankou-Kangzhuang Section of the PingSui Railway

(Nanjing) – The Nankou-Kangzhuang section of the PingSui Railway is difficult to navigate due to towering mountains and rugged terrain, so the train travels slowly. The maximum daily freight capacity is only 6,000 tons, which makes it difficult to realize the railway's potential for developing the Northwest. The Ministry of Railways has decided to bypass this section and reroute the line from Nankou via Minglongda to Kangzhuang, a total length of 120 li. The construction of the project will cost a total of 10 million yuan. It has been decided that 100,000 yuan will be allocated monthly from the railway's income for the next four years, raising half of the amount, with the remaining half being subsidized by the Ministry of Railways. The rerouting plan has been approved by the Ministry of Railways, and a team will be formed to conduct a field survey. Construction is expected to begin next spring, and the new line can be completed within two years. (Central News Agency, 23rd)

Principles for the Issuance of Railway Public Bonds

(Nanjing) – The case of the first phase of the Railway Construction Public Bonds, totaling 12 million yuan, stipulates six principles, a draft ordinance, and an attached amortization schedule. The main points of the content are: (1) The funds are stipulated to be used for consolidating old lines and building new lines. (2) The bonds will be issued in denominations of 1,000 yuan, 500 yuan, and 100 yuan. (3) The annual interest rate is 6%, which will be paid off in sixteen installments over eight years. (4) It is stipulated that the bonds will be issued by the Ministry of Railways through banks at a discount of 89% on New Year's Day this year, and principal and interest will begin to be repaid in June of next year. (5) The surplus of the national railways will be used as a guarantee for the repayment of principal and interest. (6) The fixed amount to be issued is 12 million yuan. The Central Political Committee has now approved the principles and sent the draft ordinance to the Legislative Yuan for review. (Central News Agency, 23rd)

They will be withdrawn after the formal establishment of the provincial party headquarters. Each special commissioner will have a secretary to assist in daily affairs and a design committee to plan party affairs schemes. The special commissioners will be appointed by members of the Central Committee and will only receive office expenses. (Central News Agency, 23rd)

Strange Phenomenon of Japanese Party Politics (Japanese Correspondence)

Bribery Problems Lead to Party Split

Since the opening of the 65th session of the Japanese Diet, Araki resigned due to internal control issues. As a result, the power of political parties seemed to rise, and constitutional politics seemed to have a chance to revive. However, in the midst of this, two noteworthy problems have arisen. The first is that the Minister of Education, Hatoyama Ichiro, received a bribe of 50,000 yen from brokering the sale of two stocks: the merchant Kokujin artificial silk and Kobe Steel. This has now been exposed in the Diet by Okamoto Ikki. The second is the split in the Seiyukai party, resulting from the first problem, with Tokonami Takejiro and Kuhara Fusanosuke colluding to make things difficult for Hatoyama, forcing him to resign, and creating a foundation for the cabinet's downfall.

Originally, Japanese parliamentary politics only nominally corresponded to reality during the Hara Takashi cabinet era. At that time, the European war had just ended, and the general public was eager for peaceful construction, so the zaibatsu were able to profit, and party politics got on the right track. However, since the outbreak of the world economic crisis, the advocacy of militarism has gradually risen. In particular, after Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi was assassinated in office on May 15 of the previous year, constitutional politics existed only in name, and all politics were secretly controlled by the military. The general public no longer trusts the Diet, or at least is indifferent to it. However, blind military action cannot solve the current economic difficulties, nor can it overcome the political contradictions within Japan. Therefore, the credibility of the military remains merely nominal and still contradicts the demands of the public.

The most notable example is the issue of the reorganization of the South Manchuria Railway Company. Private shareholders inevitably became panicked, and the two major political parties that relied on the Manchukuo Railway for revolving funds also felt threatened, fearing that they would be subject to great restrictions in the future and would have to completely obey the military. Therefore, when the 65th Diet session resumed after the recess, it began to attack the military to show the position of the political parties and to try to reverse the decline of the parties. However, before this issue had been formally resolved, a very serious problem arose between the Diet and the Saito cabinet. In terms of the development of the Japanese political situation, the Saito cabinet lacked real stability. Although Saito was a senior member of the naval clique and had gained the sympathy of the military, the two parties, Seiyukai and Minseito, still had some disagreements and often clashed. The budget proposal for the next year was only established after great effort within the cabinet, but a major storm in the Diet arose even before the budget proposal was passed.

This storm originated from a speech by Diet member Okamoto Ikki, exposing the government's ugliness, saying that Minister of Education Hatoyama Ichiro had received a bribe of 50,000 yen. As a result of the investigation by Minister of Justice Oyama, it was stated that (1) Hatoyama Ichiro did not have any hesitation about being prosecuted, (2) receiving 50,000 yen from Karafuto Kogyo was not based on facts, (3) in the past, there was a donation of 50,000 yen for election expenses between Ohkawa Heizaburo, president of the Karafuto (i.e., southern Sakhalin) Kogyo Company, and Hatoyama Ichiro, but it was purely a personal donation and did not constitute a crime at all. From the government's perspective alone, and in terms of the surface of the law, Hatoyama's reputation and the cabinet's credibility were probably not a problem and were temporarily preserved.

However, another problem arose, namely that Okamoto was suspected of fabricating facts, so Okamoto was ordered to be investigated to thoroughly investigate the matter. In fact, Okamoto's accusation of Hatoyama's bribery was not a simple personal action, but contained a very serious political meaning, namely that there were people within the Seiyukai who agreed with Okamoto and were engaged in a movement to overthrow the cabinet and split the party. The Seiyukai's executives believed that Okamoto's fabrication of facts was detrimental to him personally, and even more detrimental to the party, causing the credibility of parliamentary politics to be fundamentally lost. Therefore, they wanted to thoroughly investigate, and if any party members colluded with him, they would be punished with expulsion for disrupting party discipline. However, Tokonami Takejiro, among the elder statesmen, advocated caution, while Kuhara Fusanosuke secretly supported Okamoto and contacted the Minseito, Kokumin Domei, and other neutral factions to engage in the movement to overthrow the cabinet.

The Seiyukai split once after the death of Hara Takashi. After Inukai was assassinated, Suzuki succeeded as president, forming a situation of various factions vying for power. Among the potential successors to the presidency, Tokonami was among the elder statesmen, Kuhara was considered a zaibatsu, and Hatoyama Ichiro was the leading young politician. Moreover, Hatoyama was related to Suzuki Saburo by marriage and was currently a state minister, so it was very convenient for him to proceed. Therefore, the Kuhara faction and the Tokonami faction were even more determined to unite and attack him. As a result, the internal conflicts of the Seiyukai became even more severe. If it truly split, the remaining members of the Seiyukai might be reduced to around a hundred. (February 17, 1934, Tokyo)

Yan Huiqing Speaks on Sino-Soviet Relations in Peiping

Resumption of Diplomatic Relations is the First Paragraph of the Article

The Future of Diplomacy Depends on Oneself

Peiping Correspondence, Peiping Diplomatic Monthly, yesterday (20th) evening, welcomed Ambassador Yan Huiqing at the European and American Alumni Association and invited prominent figures from all walks of life to accompany him. After a simple meal, Ambassador Yan gave a speech at 8 PM on Sino-Soviet relations and the situation in the Far East. Yan first recounted the negotiations with Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov in Geneva to resume diplomatic relations. The secrecy and speed of this matter had been known to the world and need not be repeated. However, when Litvinov arrived in Geneva, diplomatic circles widely rumored that Litvinov would sign an important agreement with a certain country, and the atmosphere was quite tense. When the exchange of texts for the resumption of diplomatic relations was announced, the so-called important agreement was not with a certain country but with China, which surprised everyone. Yan said that although our country is weak, we should not underestimate ourselves too much. He recalled that when China severed relations with Germany in the sixth year of the Republic of China, the severance note from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs was delivered to the German embassy by his brother. The Germans knew that China could not send a single soldier to participate in the war, nor could it send a single warship to Europe, but the German minister's face immediately changed when he saw the note, because China had such a large territory and 400 million people. These 400 million people said that Germany was wrong and joined the front line against it, which was terrible. The significance of the Soviet Union's resumption of diplomatic relations with China this time is the same. It would be unfavorable for the Soviet Union to be enemies with 400 million people. The resumption of diplomatic relations is only the first paragraph of the article. How the subsequent articles will be written, after the resumption of diplomatic relations, there was a widespread rumor in the country that economic investigation teams and industrial investigation teams would go to Russia, but later there was no news. He had repeatedly telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to urge this matter, and now he still hopes that the people of the country will realize this matter. When the United States and Russia resumed diplomatic relations this time, he met the American ambassador in Paris, who had as many as eighty staff members, most of whom were handling commercial affairs. The Non-Aggression Pact stipulates that force cannot be used as a tool of aggression. The Soviet Union's foreign trade, buying and selling, are all state-run, and the power is very great. Whoever treats me well, I will buy their goods; whoever treats me badly, I will not buy their goods, manipulating it as desired. In foreign actions, it is no less than military force. Now American merchants are forming large groups, increasing their power, so that they are a qualified enemy to the Soviet Union's state-run trade. This point is also something that the people of the country should pay attention to. For example, tea has always been a major export to Russia. Tea merchants should now unite to form a large group. Next, he talked about the outline of the Middle East Road issue, saying that Sino-Soviet relations, in addition to the Northeast, also involve Xinjiang in the Northwest. Russia originally had the Siberian Railway, and also built a Turkestan-Siberia Railway along the Xinjiang border. Originally, there were only two roads for our country to enter Xinjiang. Now, because of the civil war, the road to the east is blocked, and only the road to the Soviet Union is accessible, so the economic power of Xinjiang Province is entirely in the hands of the Soviet Union. If they want to sell at a high price, the people of Xinjiang have nothing else to replace Russian goods. If they want to buy cheaply, the people of Xinjiang have no other place to sell their goods. Everything is manipulated by others. Therefore, from an economic point of view, Xinjiang is already in the pocket of the Soviet Union. The Soviet Union currently has no territorial desires for Xinjiang, because from an economic point of view, there is no need to occupy land, and it is also beneficial to consolidate the Han Chinese regime, because if the Han Chinese lose power, the Hui people will rise up, and the Hui people are not unified, and disputes will inevitably arise, which will lead to the activities of Siberia and the Hui people, making the Soviet Union internally uneasy. As for the future of diplomacy, it depends entirely on oneself. If one works hard, everything is hopeful; if one does not work hard, there is no way to do anything. On the one hand, the Southern Xinjiang Organization's Pseudo-Government Photography The three pieces of this film were taken after Usman left, when the turban-wearing people carried out the rebellion and organized the pseudo-government, and when they held a ceremony outside the city of Shufu to raise the pseudo-new national flag (the flag is green) in imitation of the Turkish style. (News Yesterday's Newspaper)

1. The newly released pseudo-commander (Anjiyan) Turban (name unknown)

2. 3. Two newly arrived Arabs (name unknown)

3. Qibaike Kazi (Note: "Kazi" means "Grand Akhund," who is in charge of editing news)

12. High school teacher, Arab (name unknown)

Speaking of it, nothing in China is unrelated to diplomacy. Financial management and governance all have foreign relations. But on the other hand, everything is unrelated to diplomacy. Without internal affairs, there is no diplomacy. Without improving internal affairs, there is nothing to do in diplomacy. Yan mentioned his feelings about the League of Nations, saying that the Chinese nation has always advocated peace, so in the future it must still focus on peace. China will support all institutions that maintain peace, but at the same time, it must also promote the spirit of martial arts among the people and prepare for military force, not to attack others, but to resist. Finally, he said that the national concept of the general public is weak, which is the biggest crisis in China. Therefore, he hopes that the people of the country will have a deep national concept. Yan's speech lasted for an hour. Finally, there was a free question and answer session, and everyone dispersed in joy. (21st)

Tianjin Uncovers Assassination Case

Traitors Conspire to Assassinate Ma Zhanshan, Unsuccessful

Police Detectives Arrest Five Male and Female Criminals

Tianjin Correspondence, The Special Task Force of the Hebei Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, at 7 PM on the 18th, uncovered a group of assassins bought by a certain country at Yanqing Lane, No. 46, in the British Concession. The target of their assassination was Mr. Ma Zhanshan, the national hero who resisted Japan in the Northeast. There were also several important figures in the Hebei provincial government and military. On the same day, four men and one woman were arrested, one was killed, and several others escaped. The entire case of male and female criminals was taken by the British Municipal Council for investigation. This morning, they have been extradited across the border by the Public Security Bureau. Because the case is serious, they will be sent to the Beiping Military Branch for interrogation after the fugitives are captured. The process of uncovering this case is that in December of last year, the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau received a tip that dozens of assassins dispatched from a certain country had sneaked into Tianjin, plotting to assassinate Chinese authorities and plunge the security into chaos, so that traitors and others could take the opportunity to make trouble. A few days later, a bombing incident suddenly occurred at the Public Security Bureau. The provincial, municipal, and police authorities believed that the tip was true, and ordered the Second Team of the Public Security Bureau's Special Task Force to be responsible for tracking the case in order to crack it. After more than a month, the Special Task Force had obtained clues, knowing that the assassination group was located on a certain street in a certain country's concession. Because of the protection of a certain country's forces, it was difficult to arrest them. Therefore, two police officers from the team tried to contact Ma Dianchen, the leader of the group. Ma was from Baoding, Hebei, and committed all kinds of evil. He had set up a Sumin Hospital in Tianjin, posing as the dean, but secretly doing some lawless things. A few months ago, he joined the pseudo-state and was introduced by someone to become the leader of this assassination group. The expenses and weapons were all transferred by a certain country. The condition was to kill Ma Zhanshan and be rewarded with 100,000 yuan, and to kill a certain important figure in Hebei and be rewarded with 320,000 yuan or so. After Ma Dianchen was ordered, he and his accomplices urgently sought ways to get started. Every day, he ordered his party members to disguise themselves as beggars or rickshaw pullers, patrolling in front of Ma Zhanshan's residence on No. 46 Road, intending to take the opportunity to strike. However, since Ma Zhanshan lived in the British Concession, he did not ask about the world and lived a secluded life. These people waited for an opportunity for many days but could not get started. However, they still ordered a party member every day to pretend to be a rickshaw puller, parking in front of Ma's residence to scout for news. In late February, Ma wanted to go to the Yuanxingchi bathhouse on Zhangzhuang Bridge on the border between France and England to bathe, and he had a car waiting in front of Yuanxingchi, intending to wait until Ma arrived and shoot him to death with guns. Unexpectedly, Ma had not gone for a long time due to illness. The party's plan was still not sold. The undercover Special Task Force member saw that the party was anxious and had no way to get started, so he took the opportunity to suggest that they move to the neighboring building on the back street of Ma's residence, and wait for a convenient time to act at night. Ma Dianchen thought it was true, so the Special Task Force member found a building on the back street of Ma's residence, which happened to be back-to-back with Ma's residence. After the party got the house, they decided to move in on the afternoon of the 18th. To avoid attracting the attention of foreigners, they hung up a wooden sign for an English Research Institute and planned to climb over Ma's building at about 4 AM on the 19th and throw hand-slipped grenades and box cannons at Ma's bedroom. After success, they planned to be picked up by a certain country's car to a certain boundary. The Special Task Force member learned the content and secretly reported it to the team headquarters. The team leader then asked the Public Security Bureau Director Ning Xiangnan to secretly notify Ma Zhanshan to pay attention and be vigilant. At about 5 PM on the afternoon of the 18th, the police officers of the Special Task Force were disguised and ambushed in the vicinity of No. 46 and No. 45. Some team members were disguised as rickshaw pullers, and some were disguised as electricians, all with hidden weapons to prevent the party from acting. At 5:30 PM, the first batch of party members came and were immediately captured in the rented house. By about 7 PM, five men and women had been captured. The leader, Ma Dianchen, was extremely cautious in his actions. He watched the wind from dozens of steps behind his first, second, and third batches of accomplices, and did not rush forward. When he passed the Waiqiang Bridge, he saw that there seemed to be movements ahead and was about to escape, but he was seen by the Special Task Force member ambushed by the bridge, who rushed out and hugged him. In a moment of urgency, Ma pulled out his gun and fired a shot, but unexpectedly hit himself in the side. He immediately fell to the ground. A patrolman from the British Concession caught a glimpse, went to inquire, and realized that it was the Public Security Bureau's Special Task Force handling a case. He told the police station to take the group of accomplices away. Ma Dianchen was immediately sent to the hospital. On the morning of the 19th, he died of excessive bleeding. The names of the remaining four men and one woman are Zheng Yufu, Gao Lishi, Wang Chengyun, He Yuqing, and Xue Xiancai, all in their twenties. Gao Lishi is only nineteen years old. After being arrested, hand-slipped grenades and other items were found in her trousers. The four male criminals were also equipped with pistols. Later, the Industrial Bureau cooperated with the Special Task Force to search the party's residence and found seven pistols, three hand-slips, six hundred bullets, and one portable machine gun. Ning Xiangnan has rewarded the Special Task Force with 200 yuan for their efforts in handling this case, and has ordered them to do their best to capture their remaining accomplices. It is said that there are a total of eleven people in the party responsible for the assassination of Ma Zhanshan. In addition to those who have been captured and killed, there are still five fugitives, all hiding in a certain country's concession. Ma Zhanshan has become even more reclusive because someone has harmed him. (20th)

Zhou Dynasty Coins Discovered in Rizhao County, Shandong

Sufficient for Studying the History of Ancient Overseas Trade

Jinan Correspondence, There are many ancient ruins in the coastal areas of Rizhao and Ju County in southeastern Shandong. Recently, a pottery jar of Zhou Dynasty coins, still connected and intact, was discovered in Donghaiyu Village, Rizhao County. It is said that the Provincial Library has sent personnel to purchase them from the villagers for research. According to Curator Wang Xiantang, the coastal area of Rizhao and Ju County was the land of the Li Yi during the Zhou Dynasty. At that time, commerce was prosperous, and there was already overseas trade. The bone coins unearthed in Donghai Village, Rizhao County, are indeed from the Western Zhou Dynasty. The museum will send personnel to purchase them in order to study the ancient currency system. Liang Siyong of the Institute of Historical and Philology of Academia Sinica will come to Jinan and then go to the coastal area of Rizhao and Ju County for archaeology. The purpose of his archaeology is to investigate the history of ancient overseas trade. He himself also intends to go to Qufu, Jining, Tengzhou, and Zou County to investigate the ruins and relics of the Zhou and Han dynasties for historical exploration. Because Tengzhou, Zou County, Qufu, and other counties were the states of the princes during the Zhou Dynasty, and many were the capitals of kings and marquises during the Han Dynasty, they are indeed a treasure trove of antiquities. Therefore, the scope of the investigation is predetermined to be there. (21st)

Wuhu Anhui Bank Closes

All Commercial Activities are Unprofitable

Many Shops are Closing, Leading to Widespread Unemployment

Wuhu Correspondence, Commercial activity in Wuhu has shown signs of steep decline after the Lunar New Year. The only financial institution in Anhui, Wuhu Anhui Bank, unexpectedly announced yesterday (20th) that it would cease to accept deposits and withdrawals. The bank was founded in the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, with a capital of 700,000 yuan. In recent years, it has lent out too many loans, such as more than 100,000 to the Electric Light Company, 60,000 to Zhang Hengchun Pharmacy, and several tens of thousands to a certain flour mill, which are all difficult to recover in a short period of time, and it feels that the turnover is not working. Although the branches in Shanghai and Tianjin Road, and the offices in inland Anhui such as Xuancheng, have good business, they have all been ordered to suspend business due to the relationship with the head office. The head office has also scheduled a shareholders' meeting on March 5 to make a final decision, but it is generally expected that the chances of resuming business are slim. The method for depositors and savers will also have to wait for the shareholders' meeting on March 5 to decide. It is said that there may not be a problem with a small number of sporadic savings. In addition, in terms of Qianzhuang, yesterday's values ​​were up to seven. Only a few companies, such as Yuankang, were listed, and most of them were merely show. The fact that Qianzhuang's business model is out of step with the times is a major reason, but it is also caused by the overall market decline. In Wuhu Port last year, all commercial activities were unprofitable. The authorities of various industries this year are looking at the future and cannot help but feel apprehensive. In order to survive, they have to try to tighten up. Therefore, in the past two days, the number of shop assistants who have been laid off has reached one thousand and several hundred, and the number of unemployed people is increasing day by day, and even more people are affected by their lives. This is really the biggest problem facing the current society, and it should not be ignored. (21st)

Current Financial Situation in Fujian Province

Tax Revenues Plummet Across the Board

Abolition of Lunar New Year Customs Leads to Financial Stagnation

Fuzhou Correspondence: After the suppression of the Fujian Incident, everything is in need of restoration. The financial problem should be solved first. Provincial Chairman Chen Yi and the provincial committee members have just arrived in the provincial capital and have already begun to discuss this. Therefore, the first step is to reduce administrative expenses, and the second is to act according to ability and give the people a chance to rest. Among the civilian losses during the Fujian Incident, Minhou, Nanping, Gutian, and other counties suffered the most, followed by Putian, Fuqing, Xianyou, Jinjiang, Hui'an, Longxi, and other counties. The provincial government has already ordered the county magistrates of these counties to investigate the situation in detail and report back in order to coordinate relief measures. Sun Jiazhe, the provincial committee member and concurrently director of the finance department, has not yet arrived in Fujian. Before Sun's arrival, the financial responsibilities are temporarily maintained by Xu Fu of the provincial committee. It is said that Xu stated to Provincial Chairman Chen Yi that he can only be responsible for one month.

Among the revenues, besides the various taxes collected by the Special Finance Office, the funds remitted by various counties, and the 300,000 borrowed from the Chamber of Commerce, with tens of thousands already paid, the total revenue is more than 200,000 yuan. The central government also remitted 500,000 yuan, so all agencies were able to receive ten days of February's expenses two days before the Lunar New Year's Eve. The education funds, being directly allocated by the central government, were able to receive 50%. As for the military expenses for various national armies and the temporary expenses for expanding the airfield, etc., they are also directly allocated by the central government, so fundraising is not too difficult. Although Fujian Province's finances have always been known to be difficult, when Fan Qiwu was in charge of finance, the monthly income was about 500,000 yuan, and the expenditure was about 600,000 yuan. Income and expenditure could barely offset each other. If it could be sorted out in order, it could gradually enter a bright future. Unfortunately, the pseudo-government disrupted it once, implementing a policy of draining the pond to catch all the fish. The land and grain taxes in various places were all borrowed and advanced in advance. Even various donation taxes, trust funds, public accumulation funds of various agencies, and aircraft donations that had not yet been remitted were all used. Now that the rebellion has been quelled, the wounds have not yet healed. All the various tax revenues, for various reasons, have plummeted, which cannot be restored to normal in a short period of time.

The business community in Fuzhou has not yet broken away from the old habits, and still considers the Lunar New Year's Eve as the general liquidation period for settling accounts. However, this year, the rebellion has just been quelled, and the business of various businesses has completely stagnated. Therefore, for this general settlement period, except for a few extremely reliable ones, all are determined to collect debts but not repay them. Medium and small-sized shops have completely stopped repaying term payments. Banks and money shops have had no choice but to announce the rollover of terms and exchange of notes, and specially licensed merchants plan to raise funds after the Lunar New Year. Therefore, although the business situation is not good, there are no major changes. (February 16)

Local News

Italian Aviator Hopes for Development of Aviation in China

Tea Reception for the Press Yesterday Afternoon

Detailed Account of Italy's Aviation Development

About to Go to Beijing to Meet with Chinese Authorities

Italian aviation celebrity Colonel Peinatti, to promote civil aviation development in China, piloted a two-winged light trainer aircraft at the Hongqiao Airport on the 18th of this month, performing various flight techniques, which was highly praised by all sectors. Mr. Pei then held a tea reception for the press in the lobby of the eighth floor of the Cathay Hotel on the Bund at 4 p.m. yesterday, discussing various aviation businesses. More than twenty reporters from Chinese and Western newspapers attended. The details of the conversation are recorded as follows:

Hope for Development of Aviation in China

Mr. Pei first stated that the Italian government and people have great sympathy for China. When he was in Italy, he had conversations with Zhang Xueliang, the Deputy Commander of Bandit Suppression in the Three Provinces, and others, and felt that China's future prospects were extremely promising. Since he came to China for observation this time, he has seen that the highest officials in China use airplanes for all their movements, which shows that the authorities are actively promoting the development of aviation. China has a vast land and abundant resources, and should engage in the development of civil aviation as soon as possible. It will be more convenient for China to develop aviation at this time, because in recent years, European and American countries have developed aviation quite well, and all their developments have detailed plans for China to adopt and implement. He also hopes that China will actively cultivate pilot talents to make them universal.

Developed Aviation in Europe and America

Mr. Pei also said that Italy's aviation industry, after the European War, was almost left behind due to the impact of the post-war period. Later, Prime Minister Mussolini concentrated forces from all sides and actively engaged in development, not only restoring the original state, but also making more progress than before. As for the aircraft used, all aircraft that have exceeded 2,000 hours of flight time are rebuilt, so the flight is safer. Furthermore, he has visited aircraft factories in various countries and felt that the aviation industry in all countries is making rapid progress, especially the Russian aircraft factory, which is large in scale and the best in the world, and its productivity is also very large.

Preparing to Visit Authorities in Beijing

Mr. Pei continued that after he came to China, he once went to Hangzhou to visit Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, but it was entirely a courtesy visit, and the development of aviation and other issues were not mentioned. Recently, according to Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek intends to meet with him again to discuss aviation in concrete terms. He also plans to go to Beijing in the near future to visit the government authorities, and also intends to travel to Beiping once.

Another Performance Before Leaving Shanghai

Mr. Pei finally said that he was honored to be welcomed by all sectors during this visit to China. He was very grateful for the praise given by all sectors and newspapers for the performance at Hongqiao. He will soon return to his country, but will come to China again in a month or two. The most pleasant thing about this visit to China is that he has many Chinese friends in less than a month, which he is very happy about. In order to repay the kindness of all sectors and promote aviation in general, he decided to give another performance before leaving Shanghai to return to his country.

Britain Purchases Night-Flying Aircraft from Italy

After Mr. Pei finished his report, someone asked whether it was true that China had recently ordered a large number of aircraft from Italy for the development of civil aviation. Mr. Pei replied that this was not true. However, he knew that China had recently purchased a night-flying aircraft from Italy, which was worth about 7,000 Italian gold coins.

Important Remarks by Kong Xiangxi After Arriving in Shanghai

Personal Inconvenience to Comment on the U.S. Raising Silver Prices

Issuance of Securities by Silver Syndicate Should Be Within the Scope of the Contract

Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, arrived in Shanghai at 7:30 a.m. yesterday after taking the overnight train from Beijing the night before last at 11:00 p.m., and went straight back to his private residence on West End Road to rest. Then, at 11:00 a.m., he met with reporters from various newspapers and went to work at the Central Bank at noon. The remarks of Mr. Kong are recorded as follows:

U.S. Raising Silver Prices

The Chinese government and banking community attach great importance to the U.S.'s imminent implementation of raising silver prices. When Mr. Kong met with reporters, he focused his conversation on this issue. The reporter first asked Mr. Kong for his opinion on the U.S. raising silver prices. According to Mr. Kong, the Central Government attaches great importance to the U.S. raising silver prices and is currently studying it. Before the Central Government's opinion has been determined, he, as the Minister of Finance, is not in a position to express any opinion. As for his personal opinion on this issue, he is also unwilling to express it, for fear of causing market turmoil. The reporter then asked Mr. Kong about the Central Government's opinion on temporarily approving the Eight-Nation Silver Agreement and prohibiting the export of silver. Mr. Kong replied that the Shanghai banking community's request to temporarily approve the Eight-Nation Silver Agreement is under consideration by the Central Government. As for whether the export of silver will be prohibited in the future, it is not yet time to talk about it. Finally, the reporter urged Mr. Kong to express his personal opinion on the Shanghai banking community's opposition to the U.S. raising silver prices. Mr. Kong smiled and said that he, even in his personal capacity, is not in a position to express it. The banking community's claim is to express the opinion of the association, and he is really not in a position to express his approval or disapproval before the government's policy is announced.

Shanghai Silver Syndicate Issues Securities

The Ministry of Finance previously used the Boxer Indemnity returned by Italy as collateral to borrow 44 million yuan from the Silver Syndicate organized by sixteen banks, including the Central, China, and Communications Banks. The Silver Syndicate has now decided to issue 30 million yuan in securities with this loan as collateral. When reporters met with Mr. Kong yesterday morning, they asked whether the Ministry of Finance had approved this move. Mr. Kong replied that the Shanghai Silver Syndicate's issuance of securities is acceptable as long as it is handled within the scope of the loan contract.

Modification of the Cotton-Wheat Loan Contract

The reporter also asked Mr. Kong about the outcome of canceling or modifying the U.S. cotton-wheat loan contract. Mr. Kong said that due to the sluggish domestic market, U.S. cotton and wheat that have already been shipped cannot continue to be purchased according to the original quota, and the original contract will inevitably be modified. Wei Wenbin, who is responsible for this matter in the United States, is currently consulting with the U.S. side on the modification. As for how to modify it and to what extent it has progressed, neither the U.S. side has announced it, nor is it convenient for our side to express it temporarily. It will be announced at an appropriate time.

Various Parties Discuss Raising Silver Prices

Banking Leaders Visited Kong Yesterday for Consultation

American Chamber of Commerce in China Held a Meeting Yesterday to Discuss

After the U.S. government implemented raising silver prices, the banking industry in this port telegraphed Roosevelt on the 20th to express its protest. Roosevelt has not yet responded. The American Chamber of Commerce in China also held an emergency meeting in this city yesterday to express its attitude. Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi, after arriving in Shanghai yesterday morning, was visited by banking leaders in the afternoon for important consultations. The news from all sides is recorded as follows:

Observations of the Shanghai Banking Community

Xin Sheng News Agency reported that since U.S. President Roosevelt is about to implement the policy of recoining silver coins to raise the price of silver and stimulate the purchasing power of various silver-using countries to increase exports, the banking community in this port believes that this move is deeply detrimental to China's economic position. It telegraphed Roosevelt on the 20th to request consideration and to request the Ministry of Finance to temporarily approve the Silver Agreement. As of last night, neither telegram had received a reply. Yesterday, Xin Sheng News Agency reporters interviewed important figures in the banking community. According to their observations, the main purpose of the U.S. policy of raising silver prices is to raise the price of its own silver production, promote the recovery plan, and stimulate the purchasing power of general silver-using and silver-producing countries. Whether it can be changed due to China's one-page telegram is unlikely. Although some people say that after the silver price rises, the amount of foreign debt repayments can be reduced, and the power to purchase necessary tools for developing resources, such as machinery, can be increased, which is not without benefit to our country, but it is very small compared to the losses in trade. In the future, in order to prevent excessive outflow of silver, our country will inevitably levy a silver export tax to compensate. The following are the figures for the relevant gold and silver ratio items in the central financial revenue and expenditure of 1933 to show the gains and losses of rising silver prices.

Decrease in Tariff Due to Silver Value

Among the items related to the gold and silver ratio in the central government's revenue account, only tariff is relevant. The customs gold unit for tariff collection is a virtual gold standard that is proportional to various gold standard currencies. The amount of annual income has a major relationship with the gold and silver ratio. For example, in the 1933 budget, tariff revenue was more than 35,465,700 yuan, accounting for more than 52% of the total revenue. If the silver price rises, the amount of customs gold depreciation will decrease, and the amount of revenue will decrease accordingly.

Debt and Diplomatic Expenditures

Among the items related to the gold and silver ratio in the central government's expenditure account, one is debt expenses, the second is the expenses of embassies and consulates in various countries in diplomatic expenses, and the third is the expenses of studying abroad in education expenses. According to the 1933 budget, the total debt expenses were more than 24,184,200 yuan, of which domestic debt accounted for more than 98,066,600 yuan. The total amount of diplomatic expenses was more than 10,663,000 yuan, of which there were still expenses of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. It is assumed that the full amount is the expenses of foreign embassies and consulates, which is added to the debt expenses, but it is only more than 150 million yuan, which is more than twice the difference compared to the tariff revenue of more than 350 million yuan. As for the expenses of studying abroad in education expenses, the amount is very small. Therefore, in terms of the central government's financial situation, raising the silver price may not be beneficial.

Construction and Import Volume

Furthermore, it is possible to purchase machinery, and the silver price can be cheaper after it is high. However, the bulk of goods imported by our country over the years are daily consumer goods, and the tools and raw materials used for re-production are very small in number. This can be seen from the reports of the customs and the International Trade Bureau over the years. When gold is expensive and silver is cheap, our country's emerging industries cannot compete with foreign goods. If the silver price rises, foreign goods will be cheap and dumped continuously, and the industrial and commercial enterprises run by the state will inevitably go bankrupt completely. What is the use of purchasing tools for re-production? By the time the capital is exhausted, how can we talk about construction? Therefore, raising the silver price is ultimately felt to be not worth the loss at this time.

Banking Community Visited Kong Yesterday

According to the reporter of Shen Shi News Agency, it was learned that the main leaders of the banking industry in this city visited Mr. Kong yesterday afternoon after Mr. Kong arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning to discuss how to deal with the U.S. silver policy. Regarding the issue of delaying the signing of the Silver Agreement, it is said that the government has decided to delay the signing. According to Lin Kanghou, Secretary General of the Bankers Association, the government is unlikely to have problems with delaying the signing of the Silver Agreement. Regarding other specific measures, the Bankers Association has not exchanged opinions with the government. Minister Kong's visit to Shanghai may involve personal discussions.

Qian Yongming's Opinion

According to Mr. Qian Yongming, manager of the Four Banks Savings Association, the U.S. congressmen also have two factions on the silver price issue. Those who support raising the silver price are mostly congressmen from silver-producing areas, and the representatives of the opposition are from non-silver-producing areas. The competition between the two factions is fierce. Now that the industrial faction has won, the huge outflow of silver from our country will inevitably be unavoidable. The Bankers Association telegraphed the U.S. to express its opposition, and the U.S. President has not yet replied. How to deal with it in the future depends on the development of the situation.

American Chamber of Commerce Held a Meeting Yesterday

The American Chamber of Commerce in China at No. 3 Guangdong Road convened an emergency meeting at the American General Assembly on Fuzhou Road at 5:30 p.m. yesterday to discuss U.S. President Roosevelt's issue of raising silver prices. President Ferron chaired the meeting, and more than eighty members attended. The discussion on the protest against the policy of raising silver prices by the Bankers Association of our country was quite long, and it was planned to send a long telegram to President Roosevelt to contribute opinions and ask for careful handling.

Roosevelt's Position Unchanged

According to a major figure in the banking community yesterday, U.S. President Roosevelt is carefully considering how to deal with the issue after receiving the telegram from Shanghai. Once the attitude is determined, a detailed reply telegram will arrive in Shanghai within a few days. At that time, the texts of both parties will be made public. It is expected that President Roosevelt will find it difficult to abandon his original policy and may add theoretical explanations to us. According to the current situation, there is still room for discussion.

Sharp Rise in the Market Price of Bonds on Both Roads in the British Market

The market price of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway bonds in London has risen a lot due to the solvency of the railway, especially the payment of surplus profits in 1918. The recent market price has risen to 75 pounds, while it was only 50 pounds in January last year. The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway has also soared in the London market due to solvency and has jumped to a high of 97 pounds, while it was only 64 pounds in January last year.

Shipping Association Cables the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Communications, Striving to Reclaim China's Shipping Rights

Seizing the Opportunity of Renewing Treaties with British, American, and Japanese Merchants

To Elevate National Sovereignty to Completeness

The Shanghai Shipping Trade Association recently sent a telegram to the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Communications in Nanjing, stating: "To the Honorable Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Communications, Nanjing: It is our understanding that China's shipping rights have long been encroached upon, and unfavorable treaties are the root cause of this predicament. The public has been eagerly anticipating the reclamation of these rights, and the government should take responsibility for handling this matter. Otherwise, it cannot be called a nation with complete sovereignty or a free and healthy people. The inability of legal jurisdiction to reach foreigners, the presence of concessions throughout commercial ports, and the stationing of foreign troops within our borders are all tools that weaken our nation and oppress our people. The seizure of shipping rights serves as the vanguard of aggression. Once foreign vessels gain unfettered navigation rights and foreign nationals enter the country, their numbers increase daily due to the convenience. This leads to demands for leased residential areas, and with the acquisition of these areas, they seek exemption from legal jurisdiction in peacetime and use protection as a pretext to station troops in times of conflict. The inability to govern foreigners through law, the spread of concessions in commercial ports, and the arbitrary stationing of troops within our borders are all consequences of allowing foreign vessels to navigate our coastal and inland waterways. It is evident that

Reclaiming Shipping Rights Is the Most Critical Focus of Amending Unequal Treaties. Recognizing this, our association, on the 18th day of September in the 18th year, outlined the advantages and disadvantages in detail and separately telegraphed the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the Executive and Legislative Yuan, as well as your esteemed ministry, requesting that all previously granted coastal and inland navigation rights to foreigners be reclaimed during treaty revisions. This would align with revolutionary principles and protect national sovereignty. We subsequently received your ministry's telegram stating, 'Received and noted. The reclamation of shipping rights is a key aspect of amending unequal treaties. We will propose reclaiming these rights at an opportune moment during treaty revisions to meet the public's expectations.' We also received Communication Ministry's approval No. 1907, stating, 'Received and noted. The encroachment of our nation's shipping rights has affected the national economy and the business operations of shipping merchants. This ministry has been planning the reclamation of shipping rights day and night. A proposed plan has been drafted and sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for review. Future treaty renewals with foreign countries will be carefully reviewed in conjunction with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to strive for the reclamation of shipping rights and meet the public's expectations.' According to the aforementioned telegrams, your esteemed ministry's dedication to the nation and its people is deeply appreciated. We now understand that the Sino-British and Sino-American treaties on commerce and navigation are due for renewal, and that the

Sino-Japanese Treaty Has Not Yet Been Ratified. Seizing the opportunity of treaty renewal, restoring our lost shipping rights, your esteemed ministry will surely follow the teachings of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen and alleviate the suffering of the people. Our only concern is that if a gradual approach is adopted, or if mutual benefit is used as an exchange, the resulting disaster will be even greater than before. Mutual benefit presupposes need and takes profit as the standard. Whether the needs are suitable or urgent, and whether the benefits are tangible or equal, must be carefully examined and thoroughly compared. Our nation's shipping industry is still in its infancy, and the main reason for this is the encroachment on shipping rights by foreign vessels. It is like someone who has had their house taken over by a noisy guest and is struggling to cope. To try and divide oneself to entertain the guest in his room and interact with him is impossible until the guest has left and the house is peaceful. The inability of our nation's commercial shipping to navigate the domestic waters of Europe, America, and Japan is similar. Therefore, revising treaties on the basis of mutual benefit would leave our nation's sovereignty incomplete and would be absolutely harmful and without benefit to our shipping industry. If this is not understood, then

A Major Mistake Will Be Made, Which Will Be Irreversible. Our association, deeply involved and experienced in this matter, does not shy away from elaborating in detail, and earnestly implores your esteemed ministry to pay special attention. Some say that while the number of Chinese ships has gradually increased in recent years, if shipping rights are reclaimed and all foreign vessels cease operations, our nation's coastal and inland ports may not have sufficient capacity to meet the demand, potentially hindering transportation. However, the reason our nation's commercial vessels are fewer than those of foreign countries is due to business failures, and the reason for those failures is the oppression by foreign vessels. If shipping rights can be reclaimed and only our nation's commercial vessels are allowed to operate on coastal and inland routes, business will flourish, and success can be assured. With the prospect of profitability, merchants throughout the country will invest in the shipping industry in droves. Existing companies will easily expand, and new shipping companies will emerge daily, ensuring the domestic transportation needs are met. Even in the current situation, the available Chinese ships can be allocated and supplemented to barely meet the demand, so there is no need to overthink this. In summary, abolishing unequal treaties is the teaching of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen, the doctrine of the Kuomintang, and the duty of the government and the people. We must overcome all difficulties to achieve this goal, with no room for hesitation or retreat. We earnestly implore your esteemed ministry to uphold the teachings, follow the doctrine, heed the will of the people, seize the opportunity, and thoroughly reclaim the lost shipping rights, so that the nation can be elevated to a position of complete sovereignty, and the people can be placed in a position of freedom and health. The nation will be fortunate, the people will be fortunate, and not only will the shipping industry benefit forever. In urgent anticipation of your response, the chairman of the Shanghai Shipping Trade Association, Yu Hede, respectfully bows."
